The downside is that there is no post-it note in the guest room, so it is inconvenient to write it down temporarily. In fact, it doesn't add much cost. Another disadvantage is the air conditioner. The indoor temperature of a five-star hotel in winter is 20-22 degrees. In fact, it can’t drop down to 25 degrees. Think about the experience of such a temperature covered with a thick quilt? This is not energy-saving, especially now that it is a transitional season, it should be set up properly. Open the window? There is an urban expressway outside the building, and the noise is too loud (praise the sound insulation effect of the windows is very good). In addition, the handle operation space of the washbasin faucet in the bathroom is too small, and it is inconvenient to switch the faucet.
After the customer service manager sees it, don't be sloppy.

msg:總體來説，性價比很高
也是對比了其他酒店，從價格和服務來説，希爾頓的房價還是很具性價比的。
1.早餐，種類多，味道好，也住了其他五星，除了裝修現代些，早餐雖種類多，但味道不好。個人還是比較看中早餐的，不好吃花樣多也會敗好感。
2.專業的服務，這類酒店的服務是其他四星的不具有的，態度好又專業，有住過其他非品牌連鎖差不多價位的酒店、民宿等，除了硬件好，服務真的缺乏專業性。
3.酒店裝修風格雖然比較復古，可能不是年輕人喜歡的風格，但是設施和衞生都不錯，該有的都有用着舒服。

同等價位推薦去其他酒店，這家不值。
